[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen running the `ExpanderFuzzer` harness against the Apache Commons Compress [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary, the fuzzer triggers a Java heap space exhaustion in the LZW decompression [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath. The crash is reported as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory` due to a [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates a denial-of-service–style failure when processing certain compressed [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer executed the `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` entry point with a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrafted input and crashed the process by exhausting the Java heap. The stack trace [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshows the error originates in the LZW decompression implementation of the Commons [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompress library.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is effectively a memory exhaustion vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenial of service[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer classified it as `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow`, reflecting a low-severity [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity issue where an attacker could supply a maliciously large or structured [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompressed stream to drive up memory usage until the application OOMs.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash occurs specifically in LZW table initialization [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`LZWInputStream.initializeTables`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when decompressing data via [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZCompressorInputStream`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The code path is reached through [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream`, invoked by the library’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexample application `Expander`, which in turn is called by the fuzzer harness.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The JVM recommends using a larger heap [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-Xmx1710m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to reproduce, confirming [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat the input triggers very high memory allocation.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No native code is at fault—the failure is purely in Java heap management.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for further investigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream`  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Table initialization logic and growth limits  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.z.ZCompressorInputStream`  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Construction and delegation to LZW decompression  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.CompressorStreamFactory`  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Input stream selection and wrapping logic  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – The `decompress` and `expand` methods that invoke the factory  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Entry point driving the creation of the compression streams [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto understand [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow inputs map to library calls[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInvestigating these components will provide a complete view of why certain inputs [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause unbounded memory allocation and lead to an OOM condition.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m185[0m[39m:        final int maxTableSize = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m:80[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        blockMode = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthirdByte & BLOCK_MODE_MASK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:        maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblockMode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35msetClearCode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDEFAULT_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m:80[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        blockMode = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthirdByte & BLOCK_MODE_MASK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:        maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblockMode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35msetClearCode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDEFAULT_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause and Symptoms  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The OOM arises because `ZCompressorInputStream` allows a header-derived [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`maxCodeSize` up to [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom `thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which then drives [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLZW’s `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to allocate multi‐gigabyte arrays.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Although `[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` does guard against too small [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msizes, it does *not* cap the *upper* bound, so oversized values slip through and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaust the heap.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Behavior  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid `.Z` streams use LZW code sizes in the [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m12[0m[39m range; we must continue to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccept that.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must throw a meaningful exception on unsupported or malicious inputs, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than proceed to huge allocations.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Location and Strategy  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `ZCompressorInputStream.java`, between computing `rawMax = thirdByte & [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK` and invoking `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, insert a validation step [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto enforce an upper limit.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Define a new private constant, e.g.:  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final int MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[33m...[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     with:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     final int rawMax = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrawMax < DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE || rawMax > MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mCompressorException[0m[1;39m([0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[32m"Unsupported LZW code size: "[0m[39m + rawMax[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             + [0m[32m". Must be between "[0m[39m + DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             + [0m[32m" and "[0m[39m + MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE + [0m[32m"."[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     maxCodeSize = rawMax;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures any header claiming >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits immediately fails with a [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcaught and surfaced by existing factory/fuzzer harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoiding the downstream OOM.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Defense-in-Depth [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - As an extra safeguard, you may add the same upper‐bound check at the start of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor its two‐arg overload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize > MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[32m"maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize + [0m[32m" exceeds allowed maximum of "[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             + MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This guards against future internal callers bypassing the [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZCompressorInputStream` check.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing and Side-Effects  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add unit tests feeding header bytes with `maxCodeSize` values over the limit, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mverifying a `CompressorException` is thrown.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Legitimate streams [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unaffected and decompress normally.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rejecting nonstandard code sizes early protects the JVM from unbounded memory [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation without altering valid decompression logic.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Rationale  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Spec‐compliant LZW never needs more than [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits; by enforcing a sane [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mceiling, we eliminate the denial-of-service vector.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch does not touch fuzz-harness code, utility methods, or external [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing exception‐wrapping in `CompressorStreamFactory` and example [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Expander`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will surface meaningful errors rather than OOM.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar patterns in other compressors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., XZ, Brotli[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m guard against [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious headers; this change aligns LZW with those controls.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue arises when running the ExpanderFuzzer against the Apache Commons[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompress codebase. A crafted input triggers an OutOfMemoryError in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLZWInputStream.initializeTables, causing the fuzzer to crash with a “Java heap [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspace” error.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch attempt was made to validate the LZW code size early and reject unsupported[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues. In `ZCompressorInputStream.java`, the code masked out the maximum code [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize, then added checks on the raw value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`rawMax`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throwing a [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorException` if it fell outside the supported range. In [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream.java`, a guard was added to throw an `IllegalArgumentException` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen `maxCodeSize` exceeds [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen building after applying these changes, the Maven compilation failed with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“cannot find symbol: class CompressorException” error in [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZCompressorInputStream.java`. The missing symbol indicates that the patch [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced a reference to `CompressorException` without the necessary import or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect exception type in scope, causing the build to fail and the fuzzers not to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe produced.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The ExpanderFuzzer was launched in interactive mode via libFuzzer. The harness [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mset environment variables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[33mRUN_FUZZER_MODE[0m[39m=[0m[35minteractive[0m[39m`, [0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m:import java.io.IOException;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Summary of Issues[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The recent patch for `ZCompressorInputStream` introduced a thrown [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorException` without importing it, causing a compilation failure:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     “cannot find symbol: class CompressorException”.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other compilation or runtime errors are reported after this change; thus, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe missing import is the sole blocker.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Fix[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma`, add the following import alongside the existing imports:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     import org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.CompressorException;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This import makes `CompressorException` in scope, allowing the recently added [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks on `rawMax` to compile correctly.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are needed to method signatures because `CompressorException` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextends `IOException`, and the constructor of `ZCompressorInputStream` already [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclares `throws IOException`.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `ZCompressorInputStream.java`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the import section [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjust below `package [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morg.apache.commons.compress.compressors.z;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Add:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.CompressorException;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      so that the imports look like:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.io.IOException;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.io.InputStream;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.nio.ByteOrder;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.CompressorException;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m <— [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnewly added[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Save file and re-run Maven build; `ZCompressorInputStream` should now compile[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessfully.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change only adds an import; it does not alter any logic or [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception‐handling behavior.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All previous guards on `rawMax` in the `.Z` header and in [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream.initializeTables` remain intact and will continue to guard against [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid or overly large code sizes.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and Side‐Effects[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Optimality**: Minimal change that directly addresses the compiler error [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout touching unrelated code.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Consistency**: Aligns with other compressor input streams [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`GzipCompressorInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which import and throw `CompressorException` for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat or header errors.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Side‐Effects**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m—no behavior change at runtime; the only effect is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation success.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Testing**: Existing unit and integration tests for `.Z` streams, plus [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing harnesses, should continue to operate unchanged. The new import does not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodify exception types thrown.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `mvn clean compile` to confirm no compilation failures.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the ExpanderFuzzer or other relevant fuzzers to ensure the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid-code-size guard triggers a `CompressorException` early instead of allowing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man OutOfMemoryError.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInpu[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtStream.jav[0m[1;92ma:21[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m27[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
